            <li><span style="line-height:150%; font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Shifting trend of ratio of upgrades on downgrades (credit ratio) gives insights of changing fortunes of sector</span></span></span></li>
        </ul>
        <p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><strong><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="color:red">Forecasting accuracy:</span></span></strong></span></span></p>
        <p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm"></p>
        <p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">CRISIL Research has an exemplary track record in forecasting the growth outlook across industries with a high degree of accuracy. Here are some of the examples highlighting the convergence between the forecasts of CRISIL Research and the actual trends that were observed across industries.</span></span></span></span></span></p>
        <ul style="margin-left:47px">
            <li style="text-align:justify; font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="line-height:150%"><strong><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Automobiles - </span></span></strong><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Before the beginning of fiscal 2015, we forecasted that domestic passenger vehicles sales volumes would increase by 4-6 per cent in 2014-15, and that of two wheelers would rise by 8-10 per cent. Although we erred slightly on the mix of growth between motorcycles and scooters (largely due to the poor monsoons impacting motor cycle sales), our views in respect of overall growth in these two segments were on track (4.0 per cent for passenger vehicles and 8.1 per cent for two wheelers)</span></span></span></li>
            <li style="text-align:justify; font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="line-height:150%"><strong><em><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Power -</span></span></em></strong><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%"> While the challenges faced by power generation companies because of lack of coal availability and the weak financial position of distribution companies were well known, CRISIL Research was the first to point out that subdued demand in the wake of slower GDP growth is an equally critical issue. Due to weak GDP growth and slowing industrial demand, we forecasted a steep decline in power demand growth to 1 per cent in 2013-14 from 6.5 per cent in 2012-13. In line with our expectations, power demand grew at only 0.4 per cent in 2013-14</span></span></span></li>
            <li style="text-align:justify; font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="line-height:150%"><strong><em><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Refining and marketing - </span></span></em></strong><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">For 2013-14, </span></span><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">CRISIL Research</span></span><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%"> had forecasted a sharp slowdown in demand growth of domestic petroleum products to 1-2 per cent vis-&agrave;-vis ~6 per cent demand growth in 2012-13. The actual demand growth turned out to be 0.7 per cent in 2013-14. Our forecast was in line with the actuals as we have a good hold on each of the end user sector and were able to precisely predict the trends</span></span></span></li>
            <li style="text-align:justify; font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="line-height:150%"><strong><em><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Cement -</span></span></em></strong><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%"> CRISIL Research forecasted that cement demand growth would remain subdued for the second consecutive year in 2013-14. Our demand growth estimate of 2.5 per cent was considerably lower than consensus or player estimates. Eventually, we ended the year with 2.7 per cent demand growth. Our views on profitability of players coming under severe pressure were correct. Similarly, towards the beginning of the fiscal, we forecast that demand growth would pick up to 5.5-6.0 per cent in 2014-15. The year ended with 5.2 per cent demand growth. Thus, we were directionally correct though the extent of growth in demand was a tad lower than what we had anticipated</span></span></span></li>
            <li style="text-align:justify; font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="line-height:150%"><strong><em><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Road and Highways - </span></span></em></strong><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">CRISIL Research was able to spot a trend change and correctly forecasted a steep decline in execution for National Highway projects in 2013-14. In the previous five years, execution had witnessed a steady double digit increase. Similarly, in 2014-15 also, we correctly forecast a further decline in execution, by analysing the awarding, project pipeline and execution capability of players</span></span></span></li>
            <li style="text-align:justify; font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><strong><em><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Pharmaceuticals -</span></span></em></strong><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%"> Despite the volatile regulatory environment, both on the domestic (DPCO controls on drug pricing) as well as international front (increased scrutiny and sanctions), CRISIL Research's revenue growth estimates for 2013-14 were largely in line</span></span></span></span></span></li>
        </ul>
        <p style="font-size:10pt; font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span ><span style="color:red">Approach for Industry analysis:</span></span></p>

        <h2 style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm"><span style="font-size:10pt"><span style="font-family:Arial,serif"><span style="color:#3c3c3c"><span style="color:red">Examples of some of the recent queries resolved by our Client Servicing Desk:<span></span></span></span></span></span></h2>
        <p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm"><span style="font-size:10pt"><span style="font-family:Arial,serif"><span style="color:#000000"><span style="font-size:10.0pt">Our Client Servicing Desk has resolved more than 1100 queries coming from our leading clients this year across BFSI sector. </span></span></span></span></p>
        <ul>
            <li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:10pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">New licensing system under phase III for FM radio stations, stipulates revenue sharing @ 4% in addition to the one-time fee for migration from phase II to phase III. Please share details of various expenses like staff cost, production expenses, royalty fee, operating profit margin etc. for FM players in phase III scenario</span></span></span></span></span></li>
            <li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:10pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">What is the collection track record of PGCIL under the pooling mechanism for inter-state transmission projects</span></span></span></span></span></li>
            <li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:10pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Please share the average realization (in Rs/kg) for Passenger Car Radial (PCR), Truck and Bus Radial (TBR), non-radial Truck and Bus and entire tyre industry separately</span></span></span></span></span></li>
            <li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:10pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">What will be the impact of Mines and Mineral Amendment Act, 2015 on cement sector? Please share the past 10 years trend of royalty rates for limestone?</span></span></span></span></span></li>
            <li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:10pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Based on the auction what will be the coal cost for Hindalco? What is the capacity of these mines and the distance from the plant? When will the mining start from these coal blocks won in the auction? What will be cheaper - imported coal or coal from auction?</span></span></span></span></span></li>
            <li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:10pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Please share the cement road traffic in million tonnes for the past six years? What is the average lead distance for cement -road and cement - rail? What is the average freight rate for road- cement for the past five years</span></span></span></span></span></li>
            <li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:10pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">What is the scenario of demand and supply of Polyethylene Terephthalate Resin (PET) in India?Who are the major players in it? Who are the major consumers? What are the current prices of PET? What would be the impact of fall in crude prices on it?</span></span></span></span></span></li>
            <li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:10pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Please share the financial performance (sales, OPM, Gearing and ICR) of the Indian steel players rated BBB and below over the last 5 years</span></span></span></span></span></li>
            <li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:10pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Please share (a) for how many MW has long term competitive bids called by various states in last 2-3 years? (b) How many long term PPAs (MW) signed on competitive basis in last 2-3 years?</span></span></span></span></span></li>
            <li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:10pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">What would be the impact of Chinese policy on Indian export and the new export markets for Indian yarn? What would be the current capex investment in the spinning and weaving sector by organised textile players?</span></span></span></span></span></li>
            <li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:10pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">What is the total auto finance outstanding for PVs and CVs separately from FY2011-16 on the basis of which category wise market share is getting calculated</span></span></span></span></span></li>
            <li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:10pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">What is the statistics for production and demand for each of the fertilizer products - urea, DAP, Complex, MOP, SSP, ANP, CAN, AS updated for FY 2016</span></span></span></span></span></li>
            <li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:10pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Please highlight the following 1) List of regulatory approvals required for setting of spinning and Dyeing unit in Gujarat 2) Is Import of cotton feasible option for a spinning plant in India &amp; 3) Comparative study of Man-made filers vis a vis Cotton made Garments</span></span></span></span></span></li>
        </ul>

        </ul>
        <ul style="margin-left:40px">
            <li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Access will be provided to the users on our web-based platform </span></span><a href="http://www.crisilresearch.com"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">www.crisilresearch.com</span></span></a><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">. Unique user IDs will be created by the Product Support team and training will be provided to ensure a smooth user-experience on the platform</span></span></span></span></span></li>
        </ul>
        <p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm"></p>
        <h2 style="font-size:10pt; text-align:left; font-family:Arial,serif"><span style="color:#3c3c3c"><span style="color:red">Annexure I: Introduction to CRISIL Research Services.</span></span></h2>
        <!--- <P style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:10pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,serif"><span style="color:#3c3c3c"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="color:red">A. Industry Research:</span></span></span></span></span></span></P>
<p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:9pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">CRISIL Research Services are available at </span></span><a href="http://www.crisilresearch.com"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="color:black">www.CRISILresearch.com</span></span></span></a><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">. This research platform will enable you to track the performance and outlook on industries by giving you near real-time access to data, research and analysis. We also provide our long-term and short-term future outlook on these industries and the factors that affect its performance and profitability. </span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:9pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">It will cater to your research and information requirements by providing you with Timely, Relevant and Interactive Research on:</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:9pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><strong><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">(I) Outlook</span></span></strong></span></span></span></p>
<ul style="margin-left:40px">
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Long-term demand-supply outlook - which will be evaluated twice a year and updated on the website</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Short-term outlook - we provide short-/medium-term outlook on domestic and international prices, landed costs and an update on the industries' performance and profitability.</span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ul>
<p style="margin-left:36pt; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"></p>
<p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:9pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><strong><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">(II) Indicative information/data points (as applicable for the Industry)</span></span></strong></span></span></span></p>
<ul style="margin-left:40px">
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Capacities, production, imports, exports and demand</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Key demand drivers</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Current demand-supply position</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Estimated market size</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Industry structure </span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Cost structure and profitability</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Manufacturing process &amp; technology</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Production and/or market share, by producer</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Changes in the regulatory environment and its impact on the industry</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Drivers of price changes</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Duty structure</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Global markets</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Company information/player profiles</span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ul>
<p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:9pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><strong><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">(III) Impact Analysis </span></span></strong></span></span></span></p>
<ul style="margin-left:40px">
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:9pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Events of material importance that impact the financial &amp;operational performance and competitive positioning of players across industries and which CRISIL Research believes to be of critical importance are covered in this section</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:9pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Impact notes have covered events like GST, Brexit, Union Budget, Real Estate bill etc. </span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ul>
<p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:9pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><strong><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">(IV) Research Plus:</span></span></strong></span></span></span></p>
<p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Research Plus provides valuable information and sharper insights to across 64 sectors covering the following:</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><strong><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="color:black">A. Ratings Corner:</span></span></span></strong></span></span></span></p>
<p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Ratings Corner will give you a quick and better understanding of any shift in the credit profile of a sector</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<ul style="margin-left:40px">
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Any change of the median ratings will give insight on the directional shift of the credit profile of the sector</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">The change in weighted average median rating in a sector will help the users to understand whether the changing credit profile is due to the bigger or smaller companies</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Any shifting trend of the ratio of upgrades on downgrades (credit ratio) will give insight of changing fortunes of the sector</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Under each sector the list of outstanding ratings are provided for quick and comparative view of the ratings of different companies</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">The link of rating rationale against each company will help the user to get a quick instructive view of the company</span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ul>
<p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"></p>
<p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><strong><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="color:black">B. Key news:</span></span></span></strong></span></span></span></p>
<p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">This section will help you in tracking all key news and event updates within a sector</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<ul style="margin-left:40px">
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Sector wise all important news are captured for quick and easy reference without missing any</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">The filtered news and events are picked up by CRISIL Research analysts and will help avoiding</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">news/events which are not critical</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">A 30 days archive of news will allow users to refer any critical news if missed out</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">CRISIL Research's comments on impactful news will allow the users to infer better the Implications</span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ul>
<p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"></p>
<p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><strong><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="color:black">C. Financial Aggregates:</span></span></span></strong></span></span></span></p>
<p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Financial aggregates on key parameters for each sector will help users in benchmarking companies against the sector's performance for either sanctioning loans or for monitoring a borrower</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<ul style="margin-left:40px">
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Financial aggregates are worked out at a very granular level covering 104 sub-sectors for benchmarking a company against the most appropriate industry</span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ul>
<ul style="margin-left:40px">
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Companies are carefully selected for financial aggregates to ensure a true representation of the sector thus avoiding any distortion</span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ul>
<p style="margin-left:36pt; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"></p>
<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><strong><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="color:black">D. Company Financials:</span></span></span></strong></span></span></span></p>
<p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">We have significantly augmented our coverage on companies making it an even more comprehensive research platform providing on-going information, analysis and opinion on Economy, Industries and Companies</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<ul style="margin-left:40px">
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">We are providing annual and quarterly financials of all NSE listed companies within each sector for easy and quick reference with option to export data directly to excel</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">In addition, on 150 large companies segregated sector wise, we will provide detailed report with complete analysis of business risk and financial risk. The reports will be available to users within a month of the AGM of the company and the quarterly updates will be available within 2 weeks of the release of the quarterly results</span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ul>
<p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"></p>
<p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><strong><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="color:black">E. Results Corner:</span></span></span></strong></span></span></span></p>
<p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">In today's volatile business environment, it's imperative for credit officers to stay informed in</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Advance about the likely shift of any sector's performance in the coming quarter</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<ul style="margin-left:40px">
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">We will provide sector wise performance forecast before the start of results season</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">We use incomparable sample size of more than 600 companies for the quarterly preview review of the sector</span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ul>
<p style="margin-left:36pt; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"></p>
<p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><strong><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="color:black">F. Operating Metrics:</span></span></span></strong></span></span></span></p>
<p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">To enable users to monitor any changing trend of operational parameters, we are tracking these within each sector</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<ul style="margin-left:40px">
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">The operational parameters like volumes, realisations, capacity utilisation, and raw material cost trends are provided for the bell weather companies in each sector</span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ul>
<p style="margin-left:36pt; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">These parameters are not easily available and are obtained by our analytical team from Analyst presentations, conference calls and management scripts</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"></p>
<p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:9pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><strong><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Unique features of our research delivery platform:</span></span></strong></span></span></span></p>
<p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:9pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">The information and analysis is disseminated through our near real-time delivery platform </span></span><a href="http://www.crisilesearch.com"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">www.crisilesearch.com</span></span></a><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">. Some of the key interactive features are as follows:</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<ul style="margin-left:40px">
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:9pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Video Clipping of Industry Experts- 2-3 minutes video clippings where our experts talk about topical issues or on our long term or short term views on the industry and the demand drivers for quick understanding of impact of changes in industries</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:9pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Analyst presentation- for quick reference, entire report is condensed into few slides containing our current views on the Demand-Supply, Price, Cost and Profitability</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:9pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Discovery- interactive tool for understanding regional dynamics of industries</span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ul>
<ul style="margin-left:40px">
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:9pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Thematic reports on analysis of new areas/concepts/trends across industries and coverage on niche industries</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:9pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Ask the analyst- A facility through which users of our services can interact with our sectoral experts for any analytical queries, clarifications or additional data requirements</span></span></span></span></span></li>

<div style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,serif"><span style="color:#3c3c3c"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="color:red">C. NBFC Report </span></span><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span ><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="color:red"></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></div>
<p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:9pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">The operating environment for non-banking financial companies (NBFCs) seems to be improving. With the economy on the mend, loan disbursements have picked up in most segments, funding costs are coming down, and several banks are facing capital constraints, giving these lenders a foot in the door.</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:9pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">However, competition is heating up across the board as new players enter. Will the pace of growth sustain? Will it be a secular ride, or will the earnings growth trajectory be better for some segments?This report delves deep into the fast-changing NBFC landscape. It contains CRISIL Research's perspective on the growth prospects, competitive scenario and attractiveness in <strong>10 segments</strong>where NBFCs operate.</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:9pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">The coverage includes:</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<ul style="margin-left:40px">
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:9pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Outlook on growth and risk by segment </span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:9pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Segment-wise profitability outlook, considering business growth, resource profile &amp; asset quality</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:9pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Detailed assessment of competitive positioning and market share of NBFCs in each segment</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:9pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Perspective on regulatory direction in each segment</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:9pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Profiles of 125 NBFCs, detailing key operational and financial parameters </span></span></span></span></span></li>

<div style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,serif"><span style="color:#3c3c3c"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="color:red">D. SME Report</span></span><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span ><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="color:red"></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></div>
<p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">CRISIL Research believes that the MSME sector retains its huge potential for financiers despite a tapering in the pace of growth and deterioration in asset quality seen in recent quarters. While several SME sectors are struggling to keep their head above water, there are many others that are doing well and offer enormous potential for lenders to tap. The challenge lies in identifying these sectors and the opportunities they offer. We have addressed these requirements through our <strong><em>Special report: Opportunities galore in SME loans despite growing stress</em></strong></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Sectors like pharmaceuticals, information technology, healthcare, dairy processing, engineering and food processing offer immense opportunities, particularly in the SME space. However, the quality of information available remains a key challenge. The report provides our outlook and up-to-date information on business and financial prospects across sectors and clusters. Our proprietary industry and cluster attractiveness matrices are aimed at enabling strategic decision-making.</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">We have also included an interactive tool that can assist in benchmarking across clusters and sectors. </span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,serif"><span style="color:#3c3c3c"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="color:red">E. Real Estate Report </span></span><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span ><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="color:red"></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">CRISIL Research regularly tracks the real estate sector. We have been publishing 'City Real(i)ty' - A comprehensive report on the real estate scenario in the top 11 cities. Additionally, we conduct customized studies </span></span>
<p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:9pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">to enable clients to take informed strategic decisions. CRISIL's research is based on intense primary sourcing through a series of interactions by our sector specialists with developers, market intermediaries, financing companies and large corporate houses and the use of proprietary models.</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:9pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><strong><u><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">City Real(i)ty</span></span></u></strong><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%"> reports offer an in-depth, area-wise analysis of residential, commercial office space and retail segments covering 400+ areas across 92 micro markets. The Cities covered are <strong>Mumbai, Beyond MMR region, Chennai, NCR, Ahmedabad, Kolkata, Pune, Bangalore, Chandigarh</strong>, <strong>Hyderabad</strong> and <strong>Cochin</strong></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:9pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><strong><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">The annual subscription includes:</span></span></strong></span></span></span></p>
<ul style="margin-left:40px">
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">3 Detailed Reports (once every 4 months)</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">12 monthly updates </span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Client Servicing Facility</span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ul>
<p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:9pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">The Client Servicing Facility allows our clients to interact with our analysts for any clarifications/additional information. All queries are generally serviced within 24 hours. This facility can be accessed by phone, fax or e-mail. </span></span></span></span></span></p>
<h2 style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:13pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,serif"><span style="color:#3c3c3c"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Coverage in the detailed reports:</span></span></span></span></span></span></h2>
<p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:9pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><strong><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">For residential real estate:</span></span></strong></span></span></span></p>
<ul style="margin-left:40px">
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">City-wise projections of the number of residential units likely to be absorbed over the next 3 years</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:8pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Potential demand and absorption from different income classes and buyer categories like Residents, Investors and Migrants</span></span></span></span></span></li>

EcoView</span></span><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="color:red"></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></div>
<p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:9pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><strong><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">EcoView</span></span></strong><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">, a monthly document published by CRISIL, provides a comprehensive analysis of the Indian macro-economy. It examines trends in key variables and provides rigorous forecasts based on the fundamental economic analysis. It focuses on linking macro trends and issues to micro variables like company sales, profits, and borrowing costs.</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="margin-left:0cm; margin-right:0cm; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:9pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">EcoView comprises a monthly analysis and our outlook on key aspects including:</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<ul>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:9pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Industrial Production</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:9pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Inflation (WPI, CPI)</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:9pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Money &amp; Banking (credit growth, liquidity situation)</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:9pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">Markets - Currency, Debt and Equity</span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:9pt"><span style="line-height:150%"><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif"><span style="font-size:10.0pt"><span style="line-height:150%">International Trade</span></span></span></span></span></li>
